<body>
    <h1>SaaS Business Requirements Document [BRD]</h1>
    <div class=3D"Section1">
        <p><strong>Business Requirements Document (BRD)</strong></p>
<p><strong>Project Title:</strong> Fusion Pay Integration Module for SaaS p=
latforms<br><strong>Prepared For:</strong> SaaS platforms<br><strong>Prepar=
ed By:</strong> tbi bank</p>
<hr>
<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-1.ProjectOverview">1. Proje=
ct Overview</h3>
<p>tbi bank, through its Fusion Pay platform, offers flexible consumer fina=
ncing options including POS loans, promotional 0% interest schemes, and BNP=
L (Buy Now Pay Later). The objective of this project is to develop a native=
 integration module for the MerchantPro platform that allows partner mercha=
nts to offer these financing options seamlessly within their e-commerce sto=
res.</p>
<p>When developing the module, it is essential to strictly follow the offic=
ial Fusion Pay <a href=3D"https://tbigroup.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/TSFMPU=
/pages/4053106704/API+documentation+-+Fusion+Pay" data-linked-resource-id=
=3D"4053106704" data-linked-resource-version=3D"34" data-linked-resource-ty=
pe=3D"page">API documentation </a>provided by tbi bank. This BRD is intende=
d to complement the API documentation by outlining business logic, UX expec=
tations, and integration context.</p>
<p><strong>1.1 Integration Scope &amp; Collaboration</strong></p>
<p>This Business Requirements Document (BRD) complements the official Fusio=
n Pay API documentation provided by tbi bank. All technical implementation =
must follow the logic, endpoints, parameters, and encryption guidelines def=
ined in the API documentation.</p>
<p>If any clarification or support is required during development, the tbi<=
strong> </strong>bank technical team is available to assist with implementa=
tion advice, encryption handling, testing coordination, and endpoint valida=
tion.</p>
<p>We recommend early engagement in case of any uncertainties, as this ensu=
res smooth delivery and avoids rework.</p>
<hr>
<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-2.Objectives">2. Objectives=
</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Provide a seamless integration between MerchantPro stores and tbi bank=
=E2=80=99s Fusion Pay platform.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Enable real-time financing simulations and loan applications directly fr=
om the merchant=E2=80=99s storefront and checkout pages.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Ensure full alignment with Fusion Pay=E2=80=99s Customer Journey and API=
 specifications.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Button on product page, cart and checkout as a payment method</p></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-3.CustomerJourneyAlignment"=
>3. Customer Journey Alignment</h3>
<p>Customer Journeys in Fusion Pay remain consistent, irrespective of the i=
nitial choice made on the first screen.</p>
<p><strong>Step 1:</strong></p>
<p>Commence at the Merchant Product Page, where you can either add items to=
 your basket or promptly select our plugin for instant payment processing.<=
/p>

<p><strong>Step 2:</strong></p>
<p>Next, proceed to choose your Payment Option and Loan Scheme. These optio=
ns may vary based on the merchant, and potential choices include: Standard =
POS loan, Promo POS loan (0% interest), and BNPL (0% interest).</p>

<hr>
<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-4.FunctionalRequirements">4=
. Functional Requirements</h3>
<h4 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-4.1InstallmentCalculatorInt=
egration">4.1 Installment Calculator Integration</h4>
<ul>
<li>
<p>API Endpoint: <a href=3D"https://tbigroup.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/TSFM=
PU/pages/4053106704/API+documentation+-+Fusion+Pay#GetCalculations" data-li=
nked-resource-id=3D"4053106704" data-linked-resource-version=3D"34" data-li=
nked-resource-type=3D"page">GetCalculations</a></p></li>
<li>
<p>Method: GET or POST (preferred: backend POST)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Required params: <code>reseller_code</code>, <code>reseller_key</code>, =
<code>amount</code>, <code>category_id</code> (optional)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Output: Dynamic list of loan schemes with all financial disclosures</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>Logic to cache response once per day (00:01+) or upon first call</p></li=
>
</ul>
<h4 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-4.2CheckoutandApplicationSu=
bmission">4.2 Checkout and Application Submission</h4>
<ul>
<li>
<p>API Endpoint: <a href=3D"https://tbigroup.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/TSFM=
PU/pages/4053106704/API+documentation+-+Fusion+Pay#Register-Application" da=
ta-linked-resource-id=3D"4053106704" data-linked-resource-version=3D"34" da=
ta-linked-resource-type=3D"page">Register Application</a></p></li>
<li>
<p>Method: POST only</p></li>
<li>
<p>Requirements:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>JSON payload encryption with provided key</p></li>
<li>
<p>Include all product and customer data (see API spec)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Optional fields: promo scheme preselection, success/failure redirect URL=
s, BNPL flag</p></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>
<h4 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-4.3ApplicationStatusMonitor=
ing">4.3 Application Status Monitoring</h4>
<ul>
<li>
<p>API: <a href=3D"https://tbigroup.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/TSFMPU/pages/=
4053106704/API+documentation+-+Fusion+Pay#Get-Application-Status" data-link=
ed-resource-id=3D"4053106704" data-linked-resource-version=3D"34" data-link=
ed-resource-type=3D"page">Get Application Status</a> , <a href=3D"https://t=
bigroup.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/TSFMPU/pages/4053106704/API+documentation=
+-+Fusion+Pay#Get-Application-Data" data-linked-resource-id=3D"4053106704" =
data-linked-resource-version=3D"34" data-linked-resource-type=3D"page">Get =
Application Data</a></p></li>
<li>
<p>Used to poll or receive callback updates</p></li>
<li>
<p>Integration of merchant-side endpoint <code>statusURL</code> if needed</=
p></li>
</ul>
<h4 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-4.4ExpressBuyButton(Optiona=
l/Phase2)">4.4 Express Buy Button (Optional / Phase 2)</h4>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Enable direct loan submission from product page with minimal inputs</p><=
/li>
<li>
<p>Support dynamic response with token and order_i</p></li>
</ul>
<p><strong>4.5 Popup Behavior:</strong></p>
<p>The popup container (iframe) is hidden at all times.</p>
<ol start=3D"1">
<li>
<p>Product page: After we will have the add to cart functionality then the&=
nbsp; button click will call the calculator. For example:</p></li>
</ol>
<p><a class=3D"external-link" data-card-appearance=3D"inline" href=3D"https=
://beta.tbibank.support/application/calculcator/?code=3DS333&amp;key=3Dclou=
dcart&amp;amount=3D555.12" rel=3D"nofollow">https://beta.tbibank.support/ap=
plication/calculcator/?code=3DS333&amp;key=3Dcloudcart&amp;amount=3D555.12<=
/a></p><span class=3D"confluence-embedded-file-wrapper image-center-wrapper=
 confluence-embedded-manual-size"><img class=3D"confluence-embedded-image c=
onfluence-external-resource image-center" width=3D"250" src=3D"https://beta=
.tbibank.support/application/views/assets/images/favicon-32x32.png" data-im=
age-src=3D"https://beta.tbibank.support/application/views/assets/images/fav=
icon-32x32.png" loading=3D"lazy"></span>
<p>The merchant will need to set the values: code (reseller_code), key (res=
eller_key), amount (the total amount of the product/s). We will find their =
store and return the corresponding view with the add to cart buttons.</p>
<p>On button click, this URL (<a class=3D"external-link" data-card-appearan=
ce=3D"inline" href=3D"https://beta.tbibank.support/application/calculcator/=
?code=3DS333&amp;key=3Dcloudcart&amp;amount=3D555.12" rel=3D"nofollow">http=
s://beta.tbibank.support/application/calculcator/?code=3DS333&amp;key=3Dclo=
udcart&amp;amount=3D555.12</a> ) should be placed in the iframe src, and th=
e iframe should be revealed.</p><span class=3D"confluence-embedded-file-wra=
pper image-center-wrapper confluence-embedded-manual-size"><img class=3D"co=
nfluence-embedded-image confluence-external-resource image-center" width=3D=
"250" src=3D"https://beta.tbibank.support/application/views/assets/images/f=
avicon-32x32.png" data-image-src=3D"https://beta.tbibank.support/applicatio=
n/views/assets/images/favicon-32x32.png" loading=3D"lazy"></span>
<p>On checkout: same logic for iframe, but with RegisterApplication request=
. It will again return an URL which the merchant needs to place in the ifra=
me src and reveal it, or to open new tab.&nbsp;</p>
<p><strong>4.6. </strong> <strong>Add to Cart Logic</strong></p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>When "Buy in Installments" is clicked on the product page:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>The "Continue" button should be replaced with an "Add to Cart" button an=
d the item must be automatically added to the cart if it isn=E2=80=99t alre=
ady</p></li>
<li>
<p>Upon selection of a scheme, a postMessage should be returned to the webs=
ite. For example:</p>
<p>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; targetWindow.postMessage(mess=
age, '*');</p>
<p>message =3D "{\"scheme_id\" : 472, \"downpayment\" : 0}" and the merchan=
t should take actions for adding the product to the cart or directly going =
to checkout (as in cloudcart). The received scheme_id and downpayment shoul=
d be added in RegisterApplication request later.</p></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-5.UI/UXandStylingRequiremen=
ts">5. UI/UX and Styling Requirements</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Module must be mobile responsive</p></li>
<li>
<p>UI must visually match existing MerchantPro theme styles</p></li>
<li>
<p>The "Buy in Installments" button should be available on:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Product page</p></li>
<li>
<p>Cart page</p></li>
<li>
<p>Checkout (as a payment method option)</p></li>
</ul></li>
<li>
<p>Button styling:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Must support 4 pre-defined design styles</p></li>
<li>
<p>Style selected from admin panel by the merchant, example 4 buttons from =
Woocommerce:</p></li>
</ul></li>
</ul>

<h4 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-PopupBehavior:">Popup Behav=
ior:</h4>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Clicking the Installments button on the product page opens a modal popup=
 or iframe</p></li>
<li>
<p>Inside the popup, the loan scheme should be shown OR redirect to the app=
lication form</p></li>
<li>
<p>Must support auto-close and error fallback if the service fails to load<=
/p></li>
</ul>
<hr>
<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-6.Technical&amp;SecurityCon=
siderations">6. Technical &amp; Security Considerations</h3>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Use available <a href=3D"https://tbigroup.atlassian.net/wiki/spaces/TSFM=
PU/pages/4053106704/API+documentation+-+Fusion+Pay#Example-files" data-link=
ed-resource-id=3D"4053106704" data-linked-resource-version=3D"34" data-link=
ed-resource-type=3D"page">PHP reference files </a>(<code>Cryptor.php</code>=
, <code>registerApplication.php</code>) for encryption logic</p></li>
</ul>

<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-7.Merchantadminpanelviewfie=
lds:"><strong>7. Merchant admin panel view fields:</strong></h3>
<p>The following options must be configurable from the admin panel:</p>
<ul>
<li>
<p>Reseller Code (text)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Reseller Key (text)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Encryption key (text)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Button Style (4 options)</p></li>
<li>
<p>Button on product page</p></li>
<li>
<p>Button on cart page</p></li>
<li>
<p>Min and max amount</p></li>
<li>
<p>3 types of tenors for the button: &lt;=3D5000 lv ; &lt;=3D10 000 lv ; &l=
t;=3D 30 000 lv.</p></li>
<li>
<p>Status: active or Inactive</p></li>
</ul><span class=3D"confluence-embedded-file-wrapper image-center-wrapper c=

Within the context of the <strong>=E2=80=9C=D0=A2=D0=B5=D0=BA=D1=81=D1=82 =

=BA=D0=B8 =D0=B7=D0=B0=D0=BF=D0=BE=D1=87=D0=B2=D0=B0=D1=89=D0=B8 =D0=BE=D1=
=82 {installment} =D0=BB=D0=B2. ({eur_installment} =E2=82=AC)</em></p>
<p><strong>Option 2:</strong> <em>{installments} =D0=B2=D0=BD=D0=BE=D1=81=
=D0=BA=D0=B8 =D0=BF=D0=BE {installment} =D0=BB=D0=B2. ({eur_installment} =
=E2=82=AC)</em></p>
<p>This selection will determine how the financing information is presented=
 on the button.</p>

<h3 id=3D"SaaSBusinessRequirementsDocument[BRD]-9.FinalNote">9. Final Note<=
/h3>
<p>This document is intended as a foundational reference for the developmen=
t of the Fusion Pay integration module and any additional technical clarifi=
cations, adjustments, or edge-case considerations can be discussed and alig=
ned with the tbi bank team during the implementation process.</p>
<p>We are committed to supporting SaaS platforms throughout the development=
 and testing phases and remain available for any questions or technical con=
sultations that may arise.</p>
<p>Let us work closely together to ensure the delivery of a robust, complia=
nt, and merchant-friendly solution.</p>
